{"nick":"supernaut","message":"The misconception begins with the premise that there are only so many ephemeral ports per IP. The truth is that the limit is based on the IP pair, or said another way, the client and server IPs together. A single client IP can connect to a server IP 64,000 times and so can another client IP.
